{
  "content": "const BASE = '/api'\n\nasync function request<T>(path: string, options?: RequestInit): Promise<T> {\n  const res = await fetch(`${BASE}${path}`, {\n    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n    ...options,\n  })\n  if (!res.ok) {\n    const err = await res.json().catch(() => ({ error: res.statusText }))\n    throw new Error(err.error || 'Request failed')\n  }\n  return res.json()\n}\n\nexport const api = {\n  // Tasks\n  getTasks: (params?: Record<string, string>) => {\n    const qs = params ? '?' + new URLSearchParams(params).toString() : ''\n    return request<any[]>(`/tasks${qs}`)\n  },\n  getTask: (id: number) => request<any>(`/tasks/${id}`),\n  createTask: (data: any) => request<any>('/tasks', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data) }),\n  updateTask: (id: number, data: any) => request<any>(`/tasks/${id}`, { method: 'PUT', body: JSON.stringify(data) }),\n  deleteTask: (id: number) => request<any>(`/tasks/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' }),\n  reorderTasks: (orders: { id: number; sort_order: number }[]) =>\n    request<any>('/tasks/reorder', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify({ orders }) }),\n\n  // Projects\n  getProjects: () => request<any[]>('/projects'),\n  createProject: (data: any) => request<any>('/projects', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data) }),\n  updateProject: (id: number, data: any) => request<any>(`/projects/${id}`, { method: 'PUT', body: JSON.stringify(data) }),\n  deleteProject: (id: number) => request<any>(`/projects/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' }),\n\n  // Tags\n  getTags: () => request<any[]>('/tags'),\n  createTag: (data: any) => request<any>('/tags', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data) }),\n  updateTag: (id: number, data: any) => request<any>(`/tags/${id}`, { method: 'PUT', body: JSON.stringify(data) }),\n  deleteTag: (id: number) => request<any>(`/tags/${id}`, { method: 'DELETE' }),\n\n  // Pomodoro\n  getSessions: (params?: Record<string, string>) => {\n    const qs = params ? '?' + new URLSearchParams(params).toString() : ''\n    return request<any[]>(`/pomodoro${qs}`)\n  },\n  createSession: (data: any) => request<any>('/pomodoro', { method: 'POST', body: JSON.stringify(data) }),\n  getTodayPomodoro: () => request<any>('/pomodoro/today'),\n\n  // Stats\n  getOverview: () => request<any>('/stats/overview'),\n  getTrend: (range?: number) => request<any[]>(`/stats/trend${range ? `?range=${range}` : ''}`),\n  getProjectStats: () => request<any[]>('/stats/projects'),\n  getPriorityStats: () => request<any[]>('/stats/priority'),\n  getHeatmap: (year?: number) => request<any[]>(`/stats/heatmap${year ? `?year=${year}` : ''}`),\n  getWeeklyStats: (params?: Record<string, string>) => {\n    const qs = params ?   "content": "import { create } from 'zustand'\n\ntype Theme = 'light' | 'dark'\n\ninterface ThemeStore {\n  theme: Theme\n  toggle: () => void\n  set: (theme: Theme) => void\n}\n\nconst saved = (typeof localStorage !== 'undefined' ? localStorage.getItem('whorl-theme') : null) as Theme | null\nconst prefersDark = typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches\nconst initial: Theme = saved || (prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light')\n\nexport const useThemeStore = create<ThemeStore>((set) => ({\n  theme: initial,\n  toggle: () => set((s) => {\n    const next = s.theme === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light'\n    localStorage.setItem('whorl-theme', next)\n    document.documentElement.classList.toggle('dark', next === 'dark')\n    return { theme: next }\n  }),\n  set: (theme) => {\n    localStorage.setItem('whorl-theme', theme)\n    document.documentElement.classList.toggle('dark', theme === 'dark')\n    set({ theme })\n  },\n}))\n\n// Apply initial theme\ndocument.documentElement.classList.toggle('dark', initial === 'dark')\n",

priority: number\n  due_date: string | null\n  project_id: number | null\n  parent_id: number | null\n  recurrence_rule: string | null\n  estimated_minutes: number\n  sort_order: number\n  completed_at: string | null\n  created_at: string\n  updated_at: string\n  project_name?: string\n  project_color?: string\n  project_icon?: string\n  tags?: Tag[]\n  subtasks?: Task[]\n}\n\nexport interface Project {\n  id: number\n  name: string\n  color: string\n  icon: string\n  archived: number\n  todo_count: number\n  done_count: number\n  total_count: number\n  created_at:  loading: boolean\n\n  // Filters\n  currentView: 'inbox' | 'today' | 'upcoming' | 'stats' | 'pomodoro' | 'project'\n  currentProjectId: number | null\n  searchQuery: string\n  filterStatus: string | void\n  setFilter: (key: 'status' | 'priority' | 'tag', value: any) => void\n\n  fetchTasks: () => Promise<void>\n  fetchProjects: () => Promise<void>\n  fetchTags: () => Promise<void>\n  createTask: (data: Partial<Task>) => Promise<Task>\n  updateTask: (id: number, data: Partial<Task>) => Promise<Task>\n  deleteTask: (id: number) => Promise<void>\n  toggleTask: (task: Task) => Promise<void>\n\n  createProject: (data: Partial<Project>) => Promise<Project>\n  updateProject: (id: number, data: Partial<Project>) => Promise<Project>\n  deleteProject: (id: number) => Promise<void>\n\n  createTag: (data: Partial<Tag>) => Promise<Tag>\n  deleteTag: (id: number) => Promise<void>\n}\n\nexport const useAppStore = create<AppState>((set, get) => ({\n  tasks: [],\n  projects: [],\n  tags: [],\n  loading: false,\n\n  currentView: 'inbox',\n  currentProjectId: null,\n  searchQuery: '',\n  filterStatus: null,\n  filterPriority: null,\n  filterTag: null,\n\n  setView: (view, projectId) => set({ currentView: view, currentProjectId: projectId ?? null }),\n  setSearchQuery: (q) => set({ searchQuery: q }),\n  setFilter: (key, value) => set({ [`filter${key.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}`]: value }),\n\n  fetchTasks: async () => {\n    const { currentView, currentProjectId, searchQuery, filterStatus, filterPriority, filterTag } = get()\n    const params: Record<string, string> = {}\n\n    if (searchQuery) params.search = searchQuery\n    if (filterStatus) params.status = filterStatus\n    if (filterPriority !== null) params.priority = String(filterPriority)\n    if (filterTag !== null) params.tag_id = String(filterTag)\n\n    if (currentView === 'today') {\n      const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]\n      params.due_to = today\n      params.parent_id = 'null'\n    } else if (currentView === 'upcoming') {\n      params.due_from = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]\n      params.parent_id = 'null'\n    } else if (currentView === 'project' && currentProjectId) {\n      params.project_id = String(currentProjectId)\n    } else {\n      params.parent_id = 'null'\n    }\n\n    const tasks = await api.getTasks(params)\n    set({ tasks })\n  },\n\n  fetchProjects: async () => {\n    const projects = await api.getProjects()\n    set({ projects })\n  },\n\n  fetchTags: async () => {\n    const tags = await api.getTags()\n    set({ tags })\n  },\n\n  createTask: async (data) => {\n    const task = await api.createTask(data)\n    await get().fetchTasks()\n    return task\n  },\n\n  updateTask: async (id, data) => {\n    const task = await api.updateTask(id, data)\n    await get().fetchTasks()\n    return task\n  },\n\n  deleteTask: async (id) => {\n    await api.deleteTask(id)\n    await get().fetchTasks()\n  },\n\n  toggleTask: async (task) => {\n    await api.updateTask(task.id, { status: task.status === 'done' ? 'todo' : 'done' })\n    await get().fetchTasks()\n  },\n\n  createProject: async (data) => {\n    const project = await api.createProject(data)\n    await get().fetchProjects()\n    return project\n  },\n\n  updateProject: async (id, data) => {\n    const project = await api.updateProject(id, data)\n    await get().fetchProjects()\n    return project\n  },\n\n  deleteProject: async (id) => {\n    await api.deleteProject(id)\n    await get().fetchProjects()\n  },\n\n  createTag: async (data) => {\n    const tag = await api.createTag(data)\n    await get().fetchTags()\n    return tag\n  },\n\n  deleteTag: async (id) => {\n    await api.deleteTag(id)\n    await get().fetchTags()\n  },\n}))\n",

  "content": "import { useAppStore } from '../../store'\nimport { useThemeStore } from '../../store/theme'\nimport { Search, Plus, Sun, Moon, Filter, X } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\n\nconst viewTitles: Record<string, string> = {\n  inbox: '收件箱',\n  today: '今天',\n  upcoming: '近期',\n  stats: '数据面板',\n  pomodoro: '番茄钟',\n  project: '项目',\n}\n\ninterface Props {\n  onAddTask: () => void\n}\n\nexport default function Header({ onAddTask }: Props) {\n  const { currentView, currentProjectId, projects, searchQuery, setSearchQuery, fetchTasks } = useAppStore()\n  const { theme, toggle: toggleTheme } = useThemeStore()\n  const [showFilters, setShowFilters] = useState(false)\n  const [filterStatus, setFilterStatus] = useState<string | null>(null)\n  const [filterPriority, setFilterPriority] = useState<number | null>(null)\n\n  const projectName = currentView === 'project' && currentProjectId\n    ? projects.find((p) => p.id === currentProjectId)?.name\n    : null\n\n  const title = projectName || viewTitles[currentView] || 'Whorl'\n\n  const handleSearch = (value: string) => {\n    setSearchQuery(value)\n    setTimeout(() => fetchTasks(), 100)\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <header className=\"flex items-center justify-between border-b border-border bg-surface px-6 py-4 {currentView === 'project' && currentProjectId && (\n          <span\n            className=\"rounded-full px-2.5 py-0.5 text-xs font-medium\"\n            style={{\n              backgroundColor:           项目\n          </span>\n        )}\n      </div>\n\n      <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n        {/* Search */}\n        <div className=\"relative\">\n          <Search size={16} className=\"absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-text-muted\" />\n          <input\n            type=\"text\"\n            placeholder=\"搜索任务...\"\n            value={searchQuery}\n            onChange={(e) => handleSearch(e.target.value)}\n            className=\"h-9 w-52 rounded-lg border border-border bg-bg pl-9 pr-3 text-sm text-text placeholder-text-muted outline-none transition-all duration-200 focus:w-72 focus:border-primary\"\n          />\n          {searchQuery && (\n            <button\n              onClick={() => handleSearch('')}\n              className=\"absolute right-2 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 rounded p-0.5 text-text-muted hover:text-text\"\n            >\n              <X size={14} />\n            </button>\n          )}\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Filter toggle */}\n        <button\n          onClick={() => setShowFilters(!showFilters)}\n          className={`flex h-9 w-9 items-center justify-center rounded-lg border transition-colors ${\n            showFilters ? 'border-primary bg-primary-subtle text-primary' : 'border-border text-text-muted hover:bg-surface-hover hover:text-text'\n          }`}\n        >\n          <Filter size={16} />\n        </button>\n\n        {/* Theme toggle */}\n        <button\n          onClick={toggleTheme}\n          className=\"flex h-9 w-9 items-center justify-center rounded-lg border border-border text-text-muted transition-colors hover:bg-surface-hover hover:text-text\"\n        >\n          <motion.div key={theme} initial={{ rotate: -90, opacity: 0 }} animate={{ rotate: 0, opacity: 1 }} transition={{ duration: 0.2 }}>\n            {theme === 'light' ? ''}\n                onChange={(e) => {\n                  const v = e.target.value ? parseInt(e.target.value) : null\n                  setFilterPriority(v)\n                  useAppStore.getState().setFilter('priority', v)\n                  fetchTasks()\n                }}\n                className=\"h-8 rounded-md border border-border bg-bg px-2 text-xs text-text outline-none\"\n              >\n                <option value=\"\">全部优先级</option>\n                <option value=\"0\">低</option>\n                <option value=\"1\">中</option>\n                <option value=\"2\">高</option>\n                <option value=\"3\">紧急</option>\n              </select>\n            </div>\n          </motion.div>\n        )}\n      </AnimatePresence>\n    </header>\n  )\n}\n",

{
  "content": "import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'\nimport { useAppStore } from '../../store'\nimport TaskItem from './TaskItem'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport TaskForm from './TaskForm'\nimport { Inbox, CheckCircle2, ListTodo } from 'lucide-react'\nimport type { Task } from '../../store'\n\nexport default function TaskList() {\n  const { tasks, currentView, loading } = useAppStore()\n  const [editingTask, setEditingTask] = useState<Task | null>(null)\n\n  const todoTasks = tasks.filter((t) => t.status !== 'done')\n  const doneTasks = tasks.filter((t) => t.status === 'done')\n\n  if (tasks.length === 0) {\n    return (\n      <motion.div\n        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}\n        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}\n        className=\"flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-20 text-text-muted\"\n      >\n        <div className=\"mb-4 rounded-2xl bg-surface p-6 shadow-sm\">\n          <Inbox size={48} strokeWidth={1.5} />\n        </div>\n        <p className=\"font-display text-lg font-medium\">暂无任务</p>\n        <p className=\"mt-1 text-sm\">点击右上角「新建」添加你的第一个任务</p>\n      </motion.div>\n    )\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <div mode=\"popLayout\">\n              {todoTasks.map((task, i) => (\n                <motion.div\n                  key={task.id}\n                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}\n                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}\n                  exit={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}\n                  transition={{ delay: i * 0.03 }}\n                >\n                  <TaskItem task={task} onEdit={() => setEditingTask(task)} />\n                </motion.div>\n              ))}\n            </AnimatePresence>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Done tasks */}\n      {doneTasks.length > 0 && (\n        <div>\n          <div className=\"mb-3 flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-text-muted\">\n            <CheckCircle2 size={16} />\n            已完成 · {doneTasks.length}\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"space-y-1\">\n            <AnimatePresence mode=\"popLayout\">\n              {doneTasks.map((task, i) => (\n                <motion.div\n                  key={task.id}\n                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}\n                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}\n                  exit={{ opacity: 0, x: -20 }}\n                  transition={{ delay: i * 0.03 }}\n                >\n                  <TaskItem task={task} onEdit={() => setEditingTask(task)} />\n                </motion.div>\n              ))}\n            </AnimatePresence>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {editingTask && <TaskForm task={editingTask} onClose={() => setEditingTask(null)} />}\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n",

{
  "content": "import { useAppStore } from '../../store'\nimport { Calendar, Clock, ChevronRight, ChevronDown, Trash2, AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { format, isToday, isPast, parseISO } from 'date-fns'\nimport { zhCN } from 'date-fns/locale'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'\nimport type { Task } from '../../store'\n\nconst priorityColors = ['text-priority-0', 'text-priority-1', 'text-priority-2', 'text-priority-3']\nconst priorityBg = ['bg-priority-0/10', 'bg-priority-1/10', 'bg-priority-2/10', 'bg-priority-3/10']\nconst priorityLabels = ['低', '中', '高', '紧急']\n\ninterface Props {\n  task: Task\n  onEdit: () => void\n  depth?: number\n}\n\nexport default function TaskItem({ task, onEdit, depth = 0 }: Props) {\n  const { toggleTask, deleteTask, fetchTasks } = useAppStore()\n  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false)\n  const [subtasks, setSubtasks] = useState<Task[]>([])\n  const [loadingSub, setLoadingSub] = useState(false)\n\n  const isDone = task.status === 'done'\n  const isOverdue = task.due_date && isPast(parseISO(task.due_date)) && !isDone && !isToday(parseISO(task.due_date))\n  const isDueToday = task.due_date && isToday(parseISO(task.due_date))\n\n  const loadSubtasks = async () => {\n    if (expanded) { setExpanded(false); return }\n    setLoadingSub(true)\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`/api/tasks?parent_id=${task.id}`)\n      const data = await res.json()\n      setSubtasks(data)\n    } catch {}\n    setLoadingSub(false)\n    setExpanded(true)\n  }\n\n  const handleDelete = async (e: React.MouseEvent) => {\n    e.stopPropagation()\n    if (confirm('确定删除此任务？')) {\n      await deleteTask(task.id)\n    }\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <div\n      className={`group relative rounded-xl border transition-all duration-200 ${\n        isDone\n          ? 'border-transparent bg-transparent opacity-60'\n          : 'border-transparent bg-surface hover:border-border hover:shadow-sm'\n      }`}\n      style={{ marginLeft: depth * 24 }}\n    >\n      <div className=\"flex items-start gap-3 px-4 py-3\">\n        {/* Checkbox */}\n        <input\n          type=\"checkbox\"\n          checked={isDone}\n          onChange={() => toggleTask(task)}\n          className=\"checkbox-done mt-0.5\"\n        />\n\n        {/* Content */}\n        <div className=\"min-w-0 flex-1 cursor-pointer\" onClick={onEdit}>\n          <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n            <h3\n              className={`text-sm font-medium transition-all ${\n                isDone ? 'text-text-muted line-through' : 'text-text'\n              }`}\n            >\n              {task.title}\n            </h3>\n            {isOverdue && (\n              <span className=\"flex items-center gap-0.5 rounded-full bg-danger/10 px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium text-danger\">\n                <AlertCircle size={10} /> 逾期\n              </span>\n            )}\n          </div>\n\n          {task.description && (\n            <p className=\"mt-0.5 line-clamp-1 text-xs text-text-muted\">{task.description}</p>\n          )}\n\n          <div className=\"mt-1.5 flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2\">\n            {/* Priority */}\n            <span className={`rounded-full px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium ${priorityBg[task.priority]} ${priorityColors[task.priority]}`}>\n              {priorityLabels[task.priority]}\n            </span>\n\n            {/* Due date */}\n            {task.due_date && (\n              <span className={`flex items-center gap-1 text-[11px] ${\n                isOverdue ? 'text-danger font-medium' : isDueToday ? 'text-warning font-medium' : 'text-text-muted'\n              }`}>\n                <Calendar size={11} />\n                {isDueToday ? '今天' : format(parseISO(task.due_date), 'M月d日', { locale: zhCN })}\n              </span>\n            )}\n\n            {/* Project */}\n            {task.project_name && (\n              <span\n                className=\"rounded-full px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium\"\n                style={{\n                  backgroundColor: (task.project_color || '#6366f1') + '15',\n                  color: task.project_color || '#6366f1',\n                }}\n              >\n                {task.project_icon} {task.project_name}\n              </span>\n            )}\n\n            {/* Tags */}\n            {task.tags?.map((tag) => (\n              <span\n                key={tag.id}\n                className=\"rounded-full px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[10px]\"\n                style={{ backgroundColor: tag.color + '20', color: tag.color }}\n              >\n                #{tag.name}\n              </span>\n            ))}\n\n            {/* Estimated time */}\n            {task.estimated_minutes > 0 && (\n              <span className=\"flex items-center gap-0.5 text-[11px] text-text-muted\">\n                <Clock size={11} />\n                {task.estimated_minutes}min\n              </span>\n            )}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        {/* Actions */}\n        <div className=\"flex items-center gap-1 opacity-0 transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100\">\n          <button\n            onClick={loadSubtasks}\n            className=\"rounded-md p-1.5 text-text-muted transition-colors hover:bg-surface-hover hover:text-text\"\n          >\n            {loadingSub ? (\n              <div className=\"h-4 w-4 animate-spin rounded-full border-2 border-text-muted border-t-transparent\" />\n            ) : expanded ? (\n              <ChevronDown size={16} />\n            ) : (\n              <ChevronRight size={16} />\n            )}\n          </button>\n          <button\n            onClick={handleDelete}\n            className=\"rounded-md p-1.5 text-text-muted transition-colors hover:bg-danger/10 hover:text-danger\"\n          >\n            <Trash2 size={14} />\n          </button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Subtasks */}\n      <AnimatePresence>\n        {expanded && subtasks.length > 0 && (\n          <motion.div\n            initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}\n            animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}\n            exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}\n            className=\"overflow-hidden border-t border-border-subtle\"\n          >\n            <div className=\"space-y-0.5 py-1\">\n              {subtasks.map((sub) => (\n                <TaskItem key={sub.id} task={sub} onEdit={onEdit} depth={depth + 1} />\n              ))}\n            </div>\n          </motion.div>\n        )}\n      </AnimatePresence>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n",

}

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "import { useState } from 'react'\nimport { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'\nimport { useAppStore } from '../../store'\nimport { X, Calendar, ChevronDown, Tag, Clock, Repeat, Sparkles } from 'lucide-react'\nimport type { Task } from '../../store'\n\ninterface Props {\n  task?: Task | null\n  onClose: () => void\n}\n\nexport default function TaskForm({ task, onClose }: Props) {\n  const { projects, tags, createTask, updateTask, currentProjectId } = useAppStore()\n  const isEdit = !!task\n\n  const [title, setTitle] = useState(task?.title || '')\n  const [description, setDescription] = useState(task?.description || '')\n  const [priority, setPriority] = useState(task?.priority ?? 1)\n  const [dueDate, setDueDate] = useState(task?.due_date || '')\n  const [projectId, setProjectId] = useState<number | null>(task?.project_id ?? currentProjectId)\n  const [parentId, setParentId] = useState<number | null>(task?.parent_id || null)\n  const [recurrence, setRecurrence] = useState(task?.recurrence_rule || '')\n  const [estimated, setEstimated] = useState(task?.estimated_minutes || 0)\n  const [selectedTags, setSelectedTags] = useState<number[]>(task?.tags?.map((t) => t.id) || [])\n  const [showAdvanced, setShowAdvanced] = useState(false)\n  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false)\n\n  const priorityOptions = [\n    { value: 0, label: '低', color: '#94a3b8' },\n    { value: 1, label: '中', color: '#3b82f6' },\n    { value: 2, label: '高', color: '#f59e0b' },\n    { value: 3, label: '紧急', color: '#ef4444' },\n  ]\n\n  const handleSubmit = async () => {\n    if (!title.trim()) return\n    setSubmitting(true)\n    try {\n      const data = {\n        title: title.trim(),\n        description,\n        priority,\n        due_date: dueDate || null,\n        project_id: projectId,\n        parent_id: parentId,\n        recurrence_rule: recurrence || null,\n        estimated_minutes: estimated,\n        tag_ids: selectedTags,\n      }\n      if (isEdit) {\n        await updateTask(task!.id, data)\n      } else {\n        await createTask(data)\n      }\n      onClose()\n    } finally {\n      setSubmitting(false)\n    }\n  }\n\n  const toggleTag = (id: number) => {\n    setSelectedTags((prev) => (prev.includes(id) ? prev.filter((t) => t !== id) : [...prev, id]))\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <AnimatePresence>\n      <motion.div\n        initial={{ opacity: 0 }}\n        animate={{ opacity: 1 }}\n        exit={{ opacity: 0 }}\n        className=\"fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-black/40 backdrop-blur-sm\"\n        onClick={onClose}\n      >\n        <motion.div\n          initial={{ scale: 0.95, opacity: 0, y: 20 }}\n          animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1, y: 0 }}\n          exit={{ scale: 0.95, opacity: 0, y: 20 }}\n          transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}\n          className=\"mx-4 w-full max-w-lg rounded-2xl border border-border bg-surface shadow-2xl\"\n          onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}\n        >\n          {/* Header */}\n          <div className=\"flex items-center justify-between border-b border-border px-6 py-4\">\n            <h2 className=\"font-display text-lg font-semibold\">{isEdit ? '编辑任务' : '新建任务'}</h2>\n            <button onClick={onClose} className=\"rounded-lg p-1.5 text-text-muted transition-colors hover:bg-surface-hover hover:text-text\">\n              <X size={18} />\n            </button>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Body */}\n          <div className=\"space-y-4 px-6 py-5\">\n            {/* Title */}\n            <input\n              type=\"text\"\n              placeholder=\"任务标题\"\n              value={title}\n              onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)}\n              onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey && handleSubmit()}\n              className=\"w-full rounded-xl border border-border bg-bg px-4 py-3 text-base font-medium text-text placeholder-text-muted outline-none transition-colors focus:border-primary\"\n              autoFocus\n            />\n\n            {/* Description */}\n            <textarea\n              placeholder=\"添加描述...\"\n              value={description}\n              onChange={(e) => setDescription(e.target.value)}\n              rows={2}\n              className=\"w-full resize-none rounded-xl border border-border bg-bg px-4 py-3 text-sm text-text placeholder-text-muted outline-none transition-colors focus:border-primary\"\n            />\n\n            {/* Priority */}\n            <div>\n              <label className=\"mb-1.5 block text-xs font-medium text-text-secondary\">优先级</label>\n              <div className=\"flex gap-2\">\n                {priorityOptions.map((opt) => (\n                  <button\n                    key={opt.value}\n                    onClick={() => setPriority(opt.value)}\n                    className={`flex-1 rounded-lg border-2 py-2 text-xs font-medium transition-all ${\n                      priority === opt.value\n                        ? 'border-current shadow-sm'\n                        : 'border-border text-text-muted hover:border-border'\n                    }`}\n                    style={priority === opt.value ? { borderColor: opt.color, color: opt.color, backgroundColor: opt.color + '10' } : {}}\n                  >\n                    {opt.label}\n                  </button>\n                ))}\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            {/* Due date & Project */}\n            <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 gap-3\">\n              <div>\n                <label className=\"mb-1.5 block text-xs font-medium text-text-secondary\">\n                  <Calendar size={12} className=\"mr-1 inline\" />截止日期\n                </label>\n                <input\n                  type=\"date\"\n                  value={dueDate}\n                  onChange={(e) => setDueDate(e.target.value)}\n                  className=\"w-full rounded-lg border border-border bg-bg px-3 py-2 text-sm text-text outline-none transition-colors focus:border-primary\"\n                />\n              </div>\n              <div>\n                <label className=\"mb-1.5 block text-xs font-medium text-text-secondary\">所属项目</label>\n                <select\n                  value={projectId || ''}\n                  onChange={(e) => setProjectId(e.target.value ? parseInt(e.target.value) : null)}\n                  className=\"w-full rounded-lg border border-border bg-bg px-3 py-2 text-sm text-text outline-none transition-colors focus:border-primary\"\n                >\n                  <option value=\"\">无项目</option>\n                  {projects.map((p) => (\n                    <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>{p.icon} {p.name}</option>\n                  ))}\n                </select>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n\n            {/* Tags */}\n            {tags.length > 0 && (\n              <div>\n                <label className=\"mb-1.5 block text-xs font-medium text-text-secondary\">\n                  <Tag size={12} className=\"mr-1 inline\" />标签\n                </label>\n                <div className=\"flex flex-wrap gap-1.5\">\n                  {tags.map((tag) => (\n                    <button\n                      key={tag.id}\n                      onClick={() => toggleTag(tag.id)}\n                      className={`rounded-full px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-medium transition-all ${\n                        selectedTags.includes(tag.id) ? 'ring-1 ring-offset-1 ring-offset-surface' : 'opacity-60 hover:opacity-100'\n                      }`}\n                      style={{\n                        backgroundColor: tag.color + '20',\n                        color: tag.color,\n                        ringColor: selectedTags.includes(tag.id) ? tag.color : 'transparent',\n                      }}\n                    >\n                      #{tag.name}\n                    </button>\n                  ))}\n                </div>\n              </div>\n            )}\n\n            {/* Advanced toggle */}\n            <button\n              onClick={() => setShowAdvanced(!showAdvanced)}\n              className=\"flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs font-medium text-text-muted transition-colors hover:text-primary\"\n            >\n              <Sparkles size={12} />\n              高级任务管理\n              <ChevronDown size={12} className={`transition-transform ${showAdvanced ? 'rotate-180' : ''}`} />\n            </button>\n\n            {/* Advanced fields */}\n            <AnimatePresence>\n              {showAdvanced && (\n                <motion.div\n                  initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}\n                  animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}\n                  exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}\n                  className=\"space-y-3 overflow-hidden\"\n                >\n                  <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 gap-3\">\n                    <div>\n                      <label className=\"mb-1.5 block text-xs font-medium text-text-secondary\">\n                        <Clock size={12} className=\"mr-1 inline\" />预估时间(分钟)\n                      </label>\n                      <input\n                        type=\"number\"\n                        value={estimated}\n                        onChange={(e) => setEstimated(parseInt(e.target.value) || 0)}\n                        min={0}\n                        className=\"w-full rounded-lg border border-border bg-bg px-3 py-2 text-sm text-text outline-none transition-colors focus:border-primary\"\n                      />\n                    </div>\n                    <div>\n                      <label className=\"mb-1.5 block text-xs font-medium text-text-secondary\">\n                        <Repeat size={12} className=\"mr-1 inline\" />重复规则\n                      </label>\n                      <select\n                        value={recurrence}\n                        onChange={(e) => setRecurrence(e.target.value)}\n                        className=\"w-full rounded-lg border border-border bg-bg px-3 py-2 text-sm text-text outline-none transition-colors focus:border-primary\"\n                      >\n                        <option value=\"\">不重复</option>\n                        <option value=\"daily\">每天</option>\n                        <option value=\"weekly\">每周</option>\n                        <option value=\"monthly\">每月</option>\n                      </select>\n                    </div>\n                  </div>\n\n                  {/* Subtask parent */}\n                  <div>\n {
  "content": "import { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react'\nimport { motion } from 'framer-motion'\nimport { Play, Pause, RotateCcw, Coffee, Zap, History } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { api } from '../../api'\nimport { useAppStore } from '../../store'\n\nconst WORK_MINUTES = 25\nconst BREAK_MINUTES = 5\n\nexport default function PomodoroTimer() {\n  const { tasks } = useAppStore()\n  const [mode, setMode] = useState<'work' | 'break'>('work')\n  const [secondsLeft, setSecondsLeft] = useState(WORK_MINUTES * 60)\n  const [isRunning, setIsRunning] = useState(false)\n  const [linkedTaskId, setLinkedTaskId] = useState<number | null>(null)\n  const [todayStats, setTodayStats] = useState({ sessions: 0, total_minutes: 0 })\n  const [sessions, setSessions] = useState<any[]>([])\n  const intervalRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setInterval> | null>(null)\n\n  const totalSeconds = mode === 'work' ? WORK_MINUTES * 60 : BREAK_MINUTES * 60\n  const progress = ((totalSeconds - secondsLeft) / totalSeconds) * 100\n  const minutes = Math.floor(secondsLeft / 60)\n  const seconds = secondsLeft % 60\n\n  const loadData = useCallback(() => {\n    api.getTodayPomodoro().then(setTodayStats)\n    api.getSessions({ limit: '10' }).then(setSessions)\n  }, [])\n\n  useEffect(() => { loadData() }, [loadData])\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (isRunning && secondsLeft > 0) {\n      intervalRef.current = setInterval(() => {\n        setSecondsLeft((s) => s - 1)\n      }, 1000)\n    } else if (secondsLeft === 0) {\n      setIsRunning(false)\n      // Log session\n      api.createSession({\n        task_id: linkedTaskId,\n        duration_minutes: mode === 'work' ? WORK_MINUTES : BREAK_MINUTES,\n        type: mode,\n      }).then(() => loadData())\n\n      // Switch mode\n      if (mode === 'work') {\n        setMode('break')\n        setSecondsLeft(BREAK_MINUTES * 60)\n      } else {\n        setMode('work')\n        setSecondsLeft(WORK_MINUTES * 60)\n      }\n    }\n    return () => { if (intervalRef.current) clearInterval(intervalRef.current) }\n  }, [isRunning, secondsLeft, mode, linkedTaskId, loadData])\n\n  const reset = () => {\n    setIsRunning(false)\n    setSecondsLeft(mode === 'work' ? WORK_MINUTES * 60 : BREAK_MINUTES * 60)\n  }\n\n  const switchMode = (newMode: 'work' | 'break') => {\n    setIsRunning(false)\n    setMode(newMode)\n    setSecondsLeft(newMode === 'work' ? WORK_MINUTES * 60 : BREAK_MINUTES * 60)\n  }\n\n  const circumference = 2 * Math.PI * 120\n  const strokeDashoffset = circumference - (progress / 100) * circumference\n\n  const todoTasks = tasks.filter((t) => t.status !== 'done').slice(0, 10)\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"mx-auto max-w-2xl space-y-6\">\n      {/* Mode switch */}\n      <div className=\"flex justify-center gap-2\">\n        <button\n          onClick={() => switchMode('work')}\n          className={`flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl px-5 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium transition-all ${\n            mode === 'work' ? 'bg-primary text-white shadow-lg shadow-primary/25' : 'bg-surface text-text-secondary hover:bg-surface-hover'\n          }`}\n        >\n          <Zap size={16} /> 专注\n        </button>\n        <button\n          onClick={() => switchMode('break')}\n          className={`flex items-center gap-2 rounded-xl px-5 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium transition-all ${\n            mode === 'break' ? 'bg-success text-white shadow-lg shadow-success/25' : 'bg-surface text-text-secondary hover:bg-surface-hover'\n          }`}\n        >\n          <Coffee size={16} /> 休息\n        </button>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Timer circle */}\n      <motion.div\n        initial={{ scale: 0.9, opacity: 0 }}\n        animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1 }}\n        className=\"relative mx-auto flex h-72 w-72 items-center justify-center\"\n      >\n        <svg className=\"absolute h-full w-full -rotate-90\" viewBox=\"0 0 260 260\">\n          <circle cx=\"130\" cy=\"130\" r=\"120\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"var(--color-border)\" strokeWidth=\"6\" />\n          <circle\n            cx=\"130\" cy=\"130\" r=\"120\" fill=\"none\"\n            stroke={mode === 'work' ? 'var(--color-primary)' : 'var(--color-success)'}\n            strokeWidth=\"6\"\n            strokeLinecap=\"round\"\n            strokeDasharray={circumference}\n            strokeDashoffset={strokeDashoffset}\n            className=\"transition-all duration-1000 ease-linear\"\n          />\n        </svg>\n        <div className=\"text-center\">\n          <div className=\"font-display text-6xl font-bold tracking-tight tabular-nums\">\n            {String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')}:{String(seconds).padStart(2, '0')}\n          </div>\n          <div className=\"mt-2 text-sm text-text-muted\">\n            {mode === 'work' ? '专注时间' : '休息时间'}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </motion.div>\n\n      {/* Controls */}\n      <div className=\"flex justify-center gap-3\">\n        <button\n          onClick={() => setIsRunning(!isRunning)}\n          className={`flex h-14 w-14 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl text-white shadow-lg transition-all hover:scale-105 active:scale-95 ${\n            mode === 'work' ? 'bg-primary shadow-primary/30' : 'bg-success shadow-success/30'\n          }`}\n        >\n          {isRunning ? <Pause size={24} /> : <Play size={24} className=\"ml-1\" />}\n        </button>\n        <button\n          onClick={reset}\n          className=\"flex h-14 w-14 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl border border-border bg-surface text-text-secondary transition-all hover:bg-surface-hover hover:scale-105 active:scale-95\"\n        >\n          <RotateCcw size={20} />\n        </button>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Link task */}\n      <div className=\"rounded-2xl border border-border bg-surface p-5\">\n        <label className=\"mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-text-secondary\">关联任务</label>\n        <select\n          value={linkedTaskId || ''}\n          onChange={(e) => setLinkedTaskId(e.target.value ? parseInt(e.target.value) : null)}\n          className=\"w-full rounded-lg border border-border bg-bg px-3 py-2.5 text-sm text-text outline-none transition-colors focus:border-primary\"\n        >\n          <option value=\"\">不关联</option>\n          {todoTasks.map((t) => (\n            <option key={t.id} value={t.id}>{t.title}</option>\n          ))}\n        </select>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Today stats */}\n      <div className=\"grid grid-cols-2 gap-4\">\n        <div className=\"rounded-2xl border border-border bg-surface p-5 text-center\">\n          <div className=\"font-display text-3xl font-bold text-primary\">{todayStats.sessions}</div>\n          <div className=\"mt-1 text-sm text-text-muted\">今日番茄</div>\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"rounded-2xl border border-border bg-surface p-5 text-center\">\n          <div className=\"font-display text-3xl font-bold text-primary\">{todayStats.total_minutes}</div>\n          <div className=\"mt-1 text-sm text-text-muted\">专注分钟</div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Recent sessions */}\n      {sessions.length > 0 && (\n        <div className=\"rounded-2xl border border-border bg-surface p-5\">\n          <h3 className=\"mb-3 flex items-center gap-2 font-display text-sm font-semibold text-text-secondary\">\n            <History size={16} /> 最近记录\n          </h3>\n          <div className=\"space-y-2\">\n            {sessions.slice(0, 5).map((s) => (\n              <div key={s.id} className=\"flex items-center justify-between text-sm\">\n                <span className=\"text-text\">\n                  {s.type === 'work' ? '🍅' : '☕'} {s.task_title || '未关联任务'}\n                </span>\n                <span className=\"text-text-muted\">{s.duration_minutes}min</span>\n              </div>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n",

## Assistant (Build · mimo-v2-pro · 3.7s)

_Thinking:_

The issue is with the Express v5 wildcard route. Express v5 uses a different path-to-regexp version that doesn't support `*` for catch-all routes. I need to fix the server/index.ts to use a proper wildcard pattern. In Express 5, you need to use `(.*)` or a named parameter like `/*path` or `/{*path}`.

## Assistant (Build · mimo-v2-pro · 2.7s)

_Thinking:_

In Express 5, the wildcard route `*` doesn't work. I need to use `/*splat` or `/{*splat}`. Let me fix this.

**Tool: edit**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "filePath": "/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/server/index.ts",
  "oldString": "  app.get('*', (_req, res) => {\n    res.sendFile(join(distPath, 'index.html'))\n  })",
  "newString": "  app.get('/{*splat}', (_req, res) => {\n    res.sendFile(join(distPath, 'index.html'))\n  })"
}
```

## Assistant (Build · mimo-v2-pro · 9.2s)

_Thinking:_

Now let me add the data export route and the ROADMAP.md, .gitignore, etc.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "import { Router } from 'express'\nimport db from '../db.js'\n\nconst router = Router()\n\n// Export all data as JSON\nrouter.get('/json', (_req, res) => {\n  const tasks = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM tasks ORDER BY sort_order ASC, created_at DESC').all()\n  const projects = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM projects ORDER BY created_at ASC').all()\n  const tags = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM tags ORDER BY name ASC').all()\n  const taskTags = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM task_tags').all()\n  const pomodoroSessions = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM pomodoro_sessions ORDER BY started_at DESC').all()\n\n  const data = {\n    version: '1.0.0',\n    exported_at: new Date().toISOString(),\n    data: { projects, tags, tasks, task_tags: taskTags, pomodoro_sessions: pomodoroSessions },\n  }\n\n  res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', 'attachment; filename=\"whorl-export.json\"')\n  res.json(data)\n})\n\n// Export tasks as CSV\nrouter.get('/csv', (_req, res) => {\n  const tasks = db.prepare(`\n    SELECT t.*, p.name as project_name, GROUP_CONCAT(tg.name) as tag_names\n    FROM tasks t\n    LEFT JOIN projects p ON t.project_id = p.id\n    LEFT JOIN task_tags tt ON t.id = tt.task_id\n    LEFT JOIN tags tg ON tt.tag_id = tg.id\n    GROUP BY t.id\n    ORDER BY t.sort_order ASC\n  `).all() as any[]\n\n  const headers = ['id', 'title', 'description', 'status', 'priority', 'due_date', 'project_name', 'tags', 'created_at', 'completed_at']\n  const rows = tasks.map((t) => [\n    t.id,\n    `\"${(t.title || '').replace(/\"/g, '\"\"')}\"`,\n    `\"${(t.description || '').replace(/\"/g, '\"\"')}\"`,\n    t.status,\n    t.priority,\n    t.due_date || '',\n    t.project_name || '',\n    t.tag_names || '',\n    t.created_at,\n    t.completed_at || '',\n  ])\n\n  const csv = [headers.join(','), ...rows.map((r) => r.join(','))].join('\\n')\n  const bom = '\\uFEFF' // UTF-8 BOM for Excel compatibility\n\n  res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'text/csv; charset=utf-8')\n  res.setHeader('Content-Disposition', 'attachment; filename=\"whorl-tasks.csv\"')\n  res.send(bom + csv)\n})\n\nexport default router\n",
  "filePath": "/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/server/routes/export.ts"
}
```

📖 **参考文档**：任务所需的背景资料、设计规范等\n  - 📤 **产出文档**：任务完成时应交付的文件\n- 产出文档存在即标记任务有明确完成\"终点\"\n\n#### 3. 文档变更追踪\n- 定期扫描关联文档的哈希值\n- 文档被修改后在任务详情中提示\n\n### 数据库变更 (Migration v2)\n\n```sql\nCREATE TABLE documents (\n  id          INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n  project_id  INTEGER NOT NULL,\n  name        TEXT NOT NULL,\n  file_path   TEXT NOT NULL,\n  file_type   TEXT,\n  file_size   INTEGER,\n  last_modified TEXT,\n  file_hash   TEXT,\n  description TEXT,\n  created_at  TEXT DEFAULT (datetime('now')),\n  updated_at  TEXT DEFAULT (datetime('now')),\n  FOREIGN KEY (project_id) REFERENCES projects(id) ON DELETE CASCADE\n);\n\nCREATE TABLE task_documents (\n  id          INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n  task_id     INTEGER NOT NULL,\n  document_id INTEGER NOT NULL,\n  relation    TEXT DEFAULT 'reference' CHECK(relation IN ('reference','output')),\n  created_at  TEXT DEFAULT (datetime('now')),\n  FOREIGN KEY (task_id) REFERENCES tasks(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n  FOREIGN KEY (document_id) REFERENCES documents(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,\n  UNIQUE(task_id, document_id)\n);\n\nCREATE INDEX idx_documents_project ON documents(project_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_task_documents_task ON task_documents(task_id);\nCREATE INDEX idx_task_documents_doc ON task_documents(document_id);\n```\n\n### API 新增端点\n\n```\nGET    /api/documents?project_id=:id     → 获取项目文档列表\nPOST   /api/documents                     → 添加文档元数据\nPUT    /api/documents/:id                 → 更新文档信息\nDELETE /api/documents/:id                 → 删除文档记录\nPOST   /api/documents/scan                → 扫描目录批量导入\nGET    /api/tasks/:id/documents           → 获取任务关联文档\nPOST   /api/tasks/:id/documents           → 关联文档到任务\nDELETE /api/tasks/:id/documents/:docId    → 取消关联\n```\n\n### 前端变更\n- 项目详情页 Tab 切换：任务列表 / 文档池\n- TaskForm 高级区域新增文档关联面板\n- 文档列表组件（搜索/排序/类型筛选）\n\n---\n\n## v1.2.0 (规划中)\n\n- [ ] 数据导入（从 JSON 备份恢复）\n- [ ] 任务模板\n- [ ] 快捷键支持\n- [ ] 系统托盘常驻\n",

## Assistant (Build · mimo-v2-pro · 12.0s)

_Thinking:_

I see the issue! The static file middleware is matching first. Look at the response headers:
- `Accept-Ranges: bytes`- `Cache-Control: public, max-age=0`
- `Last-Modified: Fri, 03 Apr 2026 17:49:34 GMT`This means `express.static` is serving a file. But there shouldn't be a file at `/api/export/json` in the `dist/` directory. Unless... 

Oh wait, I think the issue is that `express.static` is serving from the `dist` directory and there might be a file there. Let me check.Actually, looking at the response more carefully - it says `Content-Length: 850` which is the `index.html` file. 

The path matching is the real problem here. Express static should only serve files that actually exist at the requested path, so `/api/export/json` shouldn't resolve to anything in the dist folder. This suggests either the dist directory has an unexpected structure, or there's something about how the middleware is configured that's causing it to fall through to index.html as a fallback.

The fix is straightforward: I should make the static middleware more specific by mounting it on a distinct path prefix rather than the root, so it doesn't interfere with the API routes. serve files from the dist directory, and `/api/export/json` shouldn't exist there as a file. Unless there's some weird path resolution happening.

Let me trace through what's actually being served here. The response shows `Content-Length: 850` with `text/html` content type and `Cache-Control: public, max-age=0`, which is exactly what `index.html` would look like. But there's no catch-all route that should be returning it for this path.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "import express from 'express'\nimport { join, dirname } from 'path'\nimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url'\nimport { existsSync } from 'fs'\nimport tasksRouter from './routes/tasks.js'\nimport projectsRouter from './routes/projects.js'\nimport tagsRouter from './routes/tags.js'\nimport pomodoroRouter from './routes/pomodoro.js'\nimport statsRouter from './routes/stats.js'\nimport exportRouter from './routes/export.js'\n\nconst __dirname = dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url))\nconst app = express()\nconst PORT = 3001\n\napp.use(express.json())\n\n// API Routes (registered first, before any static serving)\napp.use('/api/tasks', tasksRouter)\napp.use('/api/projects', projectsRouter)\napp.use('/api/tags', tagsRouter)\napp.use('/api/pomodoro', pomodoroRouter)\napp.use('/api/stats', statsRouter)\napp.use('/api/export', exportRouter)\n\n// v1.1.0 placeholder routes\napp.use('/api/documents', (_req, res) => {\n  res.status(501).json({ error: '文档池功能将在 v1.1.0 中可用' })\n})\n\n// Serve static frontend in production\nconst distPath = join(__dirname, '..', 'dist')\nif (existsSync(distPath)) {\n  // Serve static assets with explicit path filtering\n  app.use((req, res, next) => {\n    // Never serve static for /api paths\n    if (req.path.startsWith('/api/')) return next()\n    express.static(distPath)(req, res, next)\n  })\n\n  // SPA fallback for non-API, non-static routes\n  app.use((req, res, next) => {\n    if (req.method !== 'GET' || req.path.startsWith('/api/')) return next()\n    res.sendFile(join(distPath, 'index.html'))\n  })\n}\n\napp.listen(PORT, '127.0.0.1', () => {\n  console.log(`\\n  🌀 Whorl server running at http://localhost:${PORT}\\n`)\n})\n",
  "filePath": "/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/server/index.ts"
}
```

---

## ✅ Whorl v1.0.0 开发完成

### 项目结构
```
whorl/
├── icon/                    # Logo 资源
│   ├── whorl.png
│   └── 核桃.png
├── server/
│   ├── index.ts             # Express 入口
│   ├── db.ts                # SQLite + 迁移系统
│   └── routes/
│       ├── tasks.ts         # 任务 CRUD + 排序
│       ├── projects.ts      # 项目管理
│       ├── tags.ts          # 标签管理
│       ├── pomodoro.ts      # 番茄钟记录
│       ├── stats.ts         # 数据统计 5 个端点
│       └── export.ts        # JSON/CSV 导出
├── src/
│   ├── main.tsx / App.tsx
│   ├── store/               # Zustand (theme + app state)
│   ├── api/                 # fetch 封装
│   └── components/
│       ├── layout/          # Sidebar + Header
│       ├── tasks/           # TaskList + TaskItem + TaskForm
│       ├── stats/           # StatsDashboard (5种图表)
│       └── pomodoro/        # PomodoroTimer
├── ROADMAP.md               # v1.1.0 文档池计划
├── .gitignore
└── package.json
```

### 启动方式
```bash
cd /home/shy/workspace/taskflow

# 开发模式（前后端热更新）
npm run dev

# 生产模式
npm run build
npm start
# → http://localhost:3001
```

### 已实现功能
| 模块 | 功能 |
|------|------|
| 任务 | CRUD、子任务、优先级4级、截止日期、重复任务、搜索筛选 |
| 项目 | 分类管理、颜色图标、归档、侧边栏统计 |
| 标签 | 多标签关联、标签筛选 |
| 番茄钟 | 25/5计时、关联任务、今日统计 |
| 数据面板 | 4指标卡片、趋势折线图、项目环形图、热力日历、优先级柱状图 |
| 界面 | 亮/暗双主题、Framer Motion 动画、响应式 |
| 导出 | JSON 全量 / CSV 任务列表 |
| 扩展 | v1.1.0 文档池预留接口(501)、数据库迁移系统 |

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "import { unlinkSync, existsSync, mkdirSync } from 'fs'\nimport { join, dirname } from 'path'\nimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url'\n\nconst __dirname = dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url))\nconst DATA_DIR = join(__dirname, 'data')\nconst DB_PATH = join(DATA_DIR, 'whorl.db')\nconst WAL_PATH = join(DATA_DIR, 'whorl.db-wal')\nconst SHM_PATH = join(DATA_DIR, 'whorl.db-shm')\n\nconsole.log('\\n🔄 正在清空 Whorl 数据库...\\n')\n\nlet removed = 0\nfor (const f of [DB_PATH, WAL_PATH, SHM_PATH]) {\n  if (existsSync(f)) {\n    unlinkSync(f)\n    console.log(`  ✗ 已删除: ${f.replace(__dirname + '/', '')}`)\n    removed++\n  }\n}\n\nif (removed === 0) {\n  console.log('  ℹ 数据库不存在，无需清理')\n}\n\nmkdirSync(DATA_DIR, { recursive: true })\nconsole.log('\\n✅ 完成。下次启动服务将自动创建全新的空数据库。\\n')\n",
  "filePath": "/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/reset-db.ts"
}

## Assistant (Build · mimo-v2-pro · 7.6s)

_Thinking:_

The user has identified 5 issues. Let me analyze and fix each one:

1. **Data sync issue** - The frontend doesn't re-fetch data when navigating between views. The `useEffect` in App.tsx only runs on mount, but when the view changes (e.g., clicking "today" or a project), `fetchTasks` needs to be called again with the new filters.

2. **"进行中" (doing) status** - The user says there's no "doing" status, only "done" and "not done". The status filter shows "待办/进行中/已完成" but there's no way to mark a task as "doing". 

I should simplify this by removing the "doing" status entirely and using a cleaner binary approach with "todo" and "done" states instead.

3. **连续天数 (streak)** - Change to cumulative days (total days with at least one task completed) instead of consecutive days.

4. **Filter status issues** - Remove "进行中" from filters since the status model is just todo/done.

5. **Sidebar navigation confusion** - Clarify what each view means:
   - 收件箱 = All tasks without a project (inbox)
   - 今天 = Tasks due today
   - 近期 = Tasks due in the future (upcoming)

Now I'm checking the actual filter behavior in the TaskList component. Looking at the today view, it should only display tasks with today's due date, but there's likely a bug in how the filter is being applied.

83:   projects: [],
84:   tags: [],

86: 
87:   currentView: 'inbox',
88:   currentProjectId: null,

90:   filterStatus: null,

99:     const { currentView, currentProjectId, searchQuery, filterStatus, filterPriority, filterTag } = get()
100:     const params: Record<string, string> = {}

103:     if (filterStatus) params.status = filterStatus

109:       params.due_to = today
110:       params.parent_id = 'null'

113:       params.parent_id = 'null'

117:       params.parent_id = 'null'
118:     }

131:     set({ tags })

28:   const checkDate = new Date()
29:   while (true) {
30:     const dateStr = checkDate.toISOString().split('T')[0]
31:     const dayDone = db.prepare(
32:       "SELECT COUNT(*) as count FROM tasks WHERE status = 'done' AND date(completed_at) = date(?)"
33:     ).get(dateStr) as any
34:     if (dayDone.count > 0) {
35:       streak++

54:   const rows = db.prepare(`
55:     SELECT date(completed_at) as date, COUNT(*) as count
56:     FROM tasks

58:     GROUP BY date(completed_at)
59:     ORDER BY date ASC
60:   `).all()

64: // Project distribution
65: router.get('/projects', (_req, res) => {
66:   const rows = db.prepare(`
67:     SELECT p.id, p.name, p.color, p.icon,
68:       COUNT(t.id) as total,
69:       SUM(CASE WHEN t.status = 'done' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as done
70:     FROM projects p
71:     LEFT JOIN tasks t ON t.project_id = p.id
72:     GROUP BY p.id
73:     HAVING total > 0
74:     ORDER BY total DESC
75:   `).all()

77: })

79: // Priority distribution

87:     ORDER BY priority ASC

## Assistant (Plan · mimo-v2-pro · 53.2s)

_Thinking:_

The user wants to add Gantt-chart-like project timeline views. They're asking where this should be placed in the UI. They suggested it could go in the "全部任务" (all tasks) view.

Let me think about the options:

1. **In the "全部任务" view** - Add a view toggle (list/kanban/gantt) within the task list area
2. **As a new sidebar item** - Add a "时间线" or "甘特图" view in the sidebar
3. **In the data panel** - But the user says the data panel is for statistics, not project management

The user's instinct is to put it in "全部任务" which makes sense - it's a different way to visualize the same task data. 

I'm leaning toward a view toggle in the task list itself, letting users switch between list, timeline, and other visualization modes. This keeps the navigation clean while giving quick access to different perspectives on the same data.

好问题。我的想法是：甘特图本质上是同一组任务数据的另一种可视化，放在"全部任务"里通过视图切换最合适，不需要增加侧边栏入口。

具体方案：

**"全部任务"视图顶部添加视图切换器**

```
┌─ 全部任务 ──────────────────────────────────┐
│  [≡ 列表]  [⏱ 时间线]        [+ 新建]       │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│                                             │
│  当前视图内容（列表 或 时间线）              │
│                                             │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**时间线视图（甘特图简化版）**

```
         4月        5月        6月
项目A  ████████░░░░
  ├─ 任务1  ████
  ├─ 任务2      ████
  └─ 任务3          ████████

项目B       ░░░░████████
  ├─ 任务4      ████
  └─ 任务5          ████████
```

- 横轴：按周/月展示时间
- 纵轴：按项目分组，项目下展示有截止日期的任务
- 条形：从创建日到截止日的时间跨度，完成的任务用实色，未完成用半透明
- 无截止日期的任务不显示在时间线中

```
task_id: ses_2ab61ffb6ffeHQTeXCAMmrZV37 (for resuming to continue this task if needed)

<task_result>
Here is my report based on the five files examined:

---

## 1. State Fields for `currentView`

**File:** `/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/src/store/index.ts` (line 53)

The `currentView` field is typed as a union literal:

```ts
currentView: 'inbox' | 'today' | 'upcoming' | 'stats' | 'pomodoro' | 'project'
```

It defaults to `'inbox'` (line 87). The setter `setView` (line 94) accepts a view and an optional `projectId`:

```ts
setView: (view: AppState['currentView'], projectId?: number | null) => void
```

Other filter-related state fields: `currentProjectId`, `searchQuery`, `filterStatus`, `filterPriority`, `filterTag`.

There is **no** `viewMode` (list vs. timeline) field in the store currently.

---

## 2. How `App` Decides Which View to Render

**File:** `/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/src/App.tsx` (lines 33-39)

The decision is a simple conditional chain inside the JSX:

```tsx
{currentView === 'stats' ? (
  <StatsDashboard />
) : currentView === 'pomodoro' ? (
  <PomodoroTimer />
) : (
  <TaskList />
)}
```

All non-`stats`, non-`pomodoro` views (`inbox`, `today`, `upcoming`, `project`) fall through to `<TaskList />`. The `fetchTasks()` action in the store handles data filtering per-view (lines 98-130 in the store), so `<TaskList />` is a generic renderer that just displays whatever tasks the store provides.

This means **a new timeline view can be inserted right here** -- either as another branch in the ternary, or more elegantly by adding a `viewMode` state and conditionally rendering `<TaskTimeline />` vs `<TaskList />` inside the existing `else` branch.

---

## 3. API Parameters Available for Date-Range Queries

**File:** `/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/server/routes/tasks.ts` (lines 8, 28-29)

The GET `/tasks` endpoint accepts these query parameters:

| Parameter | SQL Clause | Purpose |
|---|---|---|
| `status` | `t.status = ?` | Filter by todo/done |
| `project_id` | `t.project_id = ?` | Filter by project |
| `parent_id` | `t.parent_id IS NULL` or `t.parent_id = ?` | Filter top-level or subtasks |
| `priority` | `t.priority = ?` | Filter by priority level |
| **`due_from`** | `t.due_date >= ?` | **Date range start (inclusive)** |
| **`due_to`** | `t.due_date <= ?` | **Date range end (inclusive)** |
| `search` | `LIKE` on title/description | Full-text search |
| `tag_id` | Subquery on `task_tags` | Filter by tag |

The **`due_from`** and **`due_to`** parameters are exactly what a timeline/Gantt view needs to fetch tasks within a visible date range. The store already uses them for the `today` and `upcoming` views (store lines 109-119), so wiring them for a custom timeline range is straightforward.

The API also returns `due_date`, `estimated_minutes`, `created_at`, `completed_at` -- all useful for positioning bars on a Gantt chart.

---

## 4. Best Insertion Point for a View Mode Toggle

**Recommended location:** `/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/src/components/layout/Header.tsx`, in the button group at **lines 55-103** (the `<div className="flex items-center gap-2">` block).

This is where search, filter toggle, theme toggle, and the "new task" button live. A **list/timeline toggle button** fits naturally here, between the filter button and the theme toggle button. The pattern to follow is identical to the existing filter toggle button (lines 77-84) -- a 9x36px bordered icon button that highlights when active.

**Concrete plan for integration:**

1. **Store** (`src/store/index.ts`): Add a new state field:
   ```ts
   viewMode: 'list' | 'timeline'
   setViewMode: (mode: 'list' | 'timeline') => void
   ```

2. **Header** (`src/components/layout/Header.tsx`): Add a toggle button (e.g., using `List` and `GanttChart` icons from lucide-react) in the button group. Only show it when `currentView` is `inbox`, `today`, `upcoming`, or `project` (not `stats`/`pomodoro`).

3. **App.tsx** (`src/App.tsx`): Replace the fallthrough `<TaskList />` with:
   ```tsx
   : viewMode === 'timeline' ? (
     <TaskTimeline />
   ) : (
     <TaskList />
   )
   ```

4. **New component** (`src/components/tasks/TaskTimeline.tsx`): A new component that reads `tasks` from the store and renders them on a time axis. The `due_from`/`due_to` API params can be extended in `fetchTasks` to support a wider date window when in timeline mode.

---

**Summary:** The codebase is well-structured for this addition. The API already supports date-range filtering. The store just needs a `viewMode` field. The Header button group is the natural toggle location. And App.tsx's view-dispatch logic has an obvious branch point. No existing code needs to be fundamentally restructured.
</task_result>
```

## 时间线视图方案

### 定位

在"全部任务"、"今日到期"、"未来计划"、项目视图中，通过 Header 按钮切换列表/时间线两种查看模式。统计面板和番茄钟不参与切换。

### 交互设计

```
┌─ 全部任务 ──────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                           [≡ 列表] [⏱ 时间线]  [+ 新建] │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  ☐ 显示无截止日期任务                                │
│                                                     │
│       3月     4月       5月       6月                │
│  ─────┼──────┼─────────┼─────────┼──                │
│  项目A ████████████░░░░                              │
│    需求分析 ████                                     │
│    方案设计     ████                                 │
│    开发实现         ██████████                       │
│                                                     │
│  项目B       ░░░░████████████                        │
│    原型设计      ████                                │
│    视觉稿            ████████                        │
│                                                     │
│  ████ 已完成   ░░░░ 未完成                           │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 实现细节

**组件：`src/components/tasks/TaskTimeline.tsx`**

- 横轴：自动计算任务时间跨度，按周为刻度
- 纵轴：按项目分组（无项目的归入"无项目"组）
- 条形：created_at → due_date 的时间跨度
  - 已完成：实色 `bg-primary`
  - 未完成：半透明 `bg-primary/40`
  - 逾期：`bg-danger/60`
- 悬浮 Tooltip：显示任务标题、截止日期、状态
- 底部开关：「显示无截止日期任务」— 无日期任务显示为当天单日短条

**状态变更：`src/store/index.ts`**

```ts
viewMode: 'list' | 'timeline'
setViewMode: (mode: 'list' | 'timeline') => void
```

**切换按钮：`src/components/layout/Header.tsx`**

- 位置：搜索栏左侧，筛选按钮之后
- 仅在任务类视图（inbox/today/upcoming/project）中显示
- 切换到时间线模式时，`fetchTasks` 自动扩展日期范围（±3个月）以填充时间轴

**无后端变更** — 现有 API 的 `due_from`/`due_to` 参数足够支撑时间线数据查询。

81: export const useAppStore = create<AppState>((set, get) => ({

83:   projects: [],
84:   tags: [],
85:   loading: false,
86: 
87:   currentView: 'inbox',
88:   currentProjectId: null,
89:   searchQuery: '',
90:   filterStatus: null,
91:   filterPriority: null,
92:   filterTag: null,
93: 
94:   setView: (view, projectId) => set({ currentView: view, currentProjectId: projectId ?? null }),
95:   setSearchQuery: (q) => set({ searchQuery: q }),
96:   setFilter: (key, value) => set({ [`filter${key.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}`]: value }),

98:   fetchTasks: async () => {
99:     const { currentView, currentProjectId, searchQuery, filterStatus, filterPriority, filterTag } = get()
100:     const params: Record<string, string> = {}
101: 
102:     if (searchQuery) params.search = searchQuery
103:     if (filterStatus) params.status = filterStatus
104:     if (filterPriority !== null) params.priority = String(filterPriority)
105:     if (filterTag !== null) params.tag_id = String(filterTag)
106: 
107:     const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]
108: 
109:     if (currentView === 'today') {
110:       // 今日到期：截止日期正好是今天的顶级任务
111:       params.due_from = today
112:       params.due_to = today
113:       params.parent_id = 'null'
114:     } else if (currentView === 'upcoming') {
115:       // 未来计划：截止日期在明天及以后的顶级任务
116:       const tomorrow = new Date()
117:       tomorrow.setDate(tomorrow.getDate() + 1)
118:       params.due_from = tomorrow.toISOString().split('T')[0]
119:       params.parent_id = 'null'
120:     } else if (currentView === 'project' && currentProjectId) {
121:       // 项目视图：该项目下的所有任务（含子任务）
122:       params.project_id = String(currentProjectId)
123:     } else {
124:       // 全部任务：所有顶级任务
125:       params.parent_id = 'null'
126:     }
127: 
128:     const tasks = await api.getTasks(params)
129:     set({ tasks })
130:   },

133:     const projects = await api.getProjects()
134:     set({ projects })
135:   },
136: 
137:   fetchTags: async () => {
138:     const tags = await api.getTags()
139:     set({ tags })
140:   },
141: 
142:   createTask: async (data) => {
143:     const task = await api.createTask(data)
144:     await get().fetchTasks()
145:     return task
146:   },
147: 
148:   updateTask: async (id, data) => {
149:     const task = await api.updateTask(id, data)
150:     await get().fetchTasks()
151:     return task

155:     await api.deleteTask(id)

160:     await api.updateTask(task.id, { status: task.status === 'done' ? 'todo' : 'done' })

36: }

39:   id: number
40:   name: string
41:   color: string
42:   task_count?: number
43: }
44: 
45: interface AppState {
46:   // Data
47:   tasks: Task[]
48:   projects: Project[]
49:   tags: Tag[]
50:   loading: boolean
51: 
52:   // Filters
53:   currentView: 'inbox' | 'today' | 'upcoming' | 'stats' | 'pomodoro' | 'project'
54:   currentProjectId: number | null
55:   searchQuery: string
56:   filterStatus: string | null
57:   filterPriority: number | null
58:   filterTag: number | null
59: 
60:   // Actions
61:   setView: (view: AppState['currentView'], projectId?: number | null) => void
62:   setSearchQuery: (q: string) => void
63:   setFilter: (key: 'status' | 'priority' | 'tag', value: any) => void
64: 
65:   fetchTasks: () => Promise<void>
66:   fetchProjects: () => Promise<void>
67:   fetchTags: () => Promise<void>

71:   toggleTask: (task: Task) => Promise<void>
72:

75:   deleteProject: (id: number) => Promise<void>
76: 
77:   createTag: (data: Partial<Tag>) => Promise<Tag>
78:   deleteTag: (id: number) => Promise<void>
79: }
80: 
81: export const useAppStore = create<AppState>((set, get) => ({
82:   tasks: [],
83:   projects: [],
84:   tags: [],
85:   loading: false,
86: 
87:   currentView: 'inbox',
88:   currentProjectId: null,
89:   searchQuery: '',
90:   filterStatus: null,
91:   filterPriority: null,
92:   filterTag: null,
93: 
94:   setView: (view, projectId) => set({ currentView: view, currentProjectId: projectId ?? null }),
95:   setSearchQuery: (q) => set({ searchQuery: q }),
96:   setFilter: (key, value) => set({ [`filter${key.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + key.slice(1)}`]: value }),
97: 
98:   fetchTasks: async () => {
99:     const { currentView, currentProjectId, searchQuery, filterStatus, filterPriority, filterTag } = get()
100:     const params: Record<string, string> = {}
101: 
102:     if (searchQuery) params.search = searchQuery
103:     if (filterStatus) params.status = filterStatus
104:     if (filterPriority !== null) params.priority = String(filterPriority)
105:     if (filterTag !== null) params.tag_id = String(filterTag)
106: 
107:     const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]
108: 
109:     if (currentView === 'today') {
110:       // 今日到期：截止日期正好是今天的顶级任务
111:       params.due_from = today
112:       params.due_to = today
113:       params.parent_id = 'null'
114:     } else if (currentView === 'upcoming') {
115:       // 未来计划：截止日期在明天及以后的顶级任务
116:       const tomorrow = new Date()
117:       tomorrow.setDate(tomorrow.getDate() + 1)
118:       params.due_from = tomorrow.toISOString().split('T')[0]
119:       params.parent_id = 'null'
120:     } else if (currentView === 'project' && currentProjectId) {
121:       // 项目视图：该项目下的所有任务（含子任务）
122:       params.project_id = String(currentProjectId)
123:     } else {
124:       // 全部任务：所有顶级任务
125:       params.parent_id = 'null'
126:     }
127: 
128:     const tasks = await api.getTasks(params)
129:     set({ tasks })
130:   },
131: 
132:   fetchProjects: async () => {
133:     const projects = await api.getProjects()
134:     set({ projects })
135:   },
136: 
137:   fetchTags: async () => {
138:     const tags = await api.getTags()
139:     set({ tags })
140:   },
141: 
142:   createTask: async (data) => {
143:     const task = await api.createTask(data)
144:     await get().fetchTasks()
145:     return task
146:   },
147: 
148:   updateTask: async (id, data) => {
149:     const task = await api.updateTask(id, data)
150:     await get().fetchTasks()
151:     return task
152:   },
153: 
154:   deleteTask: async (id) => {
155:     await api.deleteTask(id)
156:     await get().fetchTasks()
157:   },
158: 
159:   toggleTask: async (task) => {
160:     await api.updateTask(task.id, { status: task.status === 'done' ? 'todo' : 'done' })
161:     await get().fetchTasks()
162:   },
163: 
164:   createProject: async (data) => {
165:     const project = await api.createProject(data)
166:     await get().fetchProjects()
167:     return project

## Assistant (Build · mimo-v2-pro · 28.4s)

_Thinking:_

Now let me create the TaskTimeline component. This needs to:

1. Read tasks from the store
2. Group tasks by project
3. Calculate a time axis (weeks)
4. Render bars for each task based on created_at → due_date
5. Show completed vs incomplete state
6. Have a toggle to show/hide tasks without due dates
7. Support hover tooltips

Let me design this carefully.

**Tool: write**

**Input:**
```json
{
  "content": "import { useMemo, useState } from 'react'\nimport { useAppStore, type Task } from '../../store'\nimport { format, parseISO, differenceInDays, addDays, startOfWeek, eachWeekOfInterval, isToday, isPast } from 'date-fns'\nimport { zhCN } from 'date-fns/locale'\nimport { motion } from 'framer-motion'\nimport { CalendarOff, CheckCircle2, Circle, AlertCircle } from 'lucide-react'\n\ninterface GroupedProject {\n  name: string\n  color: string\n  icon: string\n  tasks: Task[]\n}\n\nconst PRIORITY_COLORS = ['#94a3b8', '#3b82f6', '#f59e0b', '#ef4444']\n\nexport default function TaskTimeline() {\n  const { tasks, timelineShowNoDate, setTimelineShowNoDate, toggleTask } = useAppStore()\n\n  // Filter: only tasks with due_date, unless toggle is on\n  const timelineTasks = useMemo(() => {\n    if (timelineShowNoDate) return tasks\n    return tasks.filter((t) => t.due_date)\n  }, [tasks, timelineShowNoDate])\n\n  // Calculate date range for the axis\n  const { axisStart, axisEnd, totalDays } = useMemo(() => {\n    const today = new Date()\n    const withDates = tasks.filter((t) => t.due_date)\n    if (withDates.length === 0) {\n      const start = addDays(today, -14)\n      const end = addDays(today, 90)\n      return { axisStart: start, axisEnd: end, totalDays: differenceInDays(end, start) }\n    }\n\n    let minDate = today\n    let maxDate = addDays(today, 30)\n    for (const t of withDates) {\n      const created = parseISO(t.created_at)\n      const due = parseISO(t.due_date!)\n      if (created < minDate) minDate = created\n      if (due > maxDate) maxDate = due\n    }\n    // Add padding\n    minDate = addDays(minDate, -7)\n    maxDate = addDays(maxDate, 14)\n    return { axisStart: minDate, axisEnd: maxDate, totalDays: differenceInDays(maxDate, minDate) }\n  }, [tasks])\n\n  // Generate week markers\n  const weeks = useMemo(() => {\n    return eachWeekOfInterval({ start: axisStart, end: axisEnd }, { weekStartsOn: 1 })\n  }, [axisStart, axisEnd])\n\n  // Group tasks by project\n  const groups = useMemo(() => {\n    const map = new Map<string, GroupedProject>()\n    for (const task of timelineTasks) {\n      const key = task.project_id ? `p${task.project_id}` : 'none'\n      if (!map.has(key)) {\n        map.set(key, {\n          name: task.project_name || '无项目',\n          color: task.project_color || '#94a3b8',\n          icon: task.project_icon || '📋',\n          tasks: [],\n        })\n      }\n      map.get(key)!.tasks.push(task)\n    }\n    return Array.from(map.values())\n  }, [timelineTasks])\n\n  const getBarStyle = (task: Task) => {\n    const startDate = parseISO(task.created_at)\n    const endDate = task.due_date ? parseISO(task.due_date) : axisStart\n    const left = Math.max(0, (differenceInDays(startDate, axisStart) / totalDays) * 100)\n    const width = Math.max(1.5, (differenceInDays(endDate, startDate) / totalDays) * 100)\n    return { left: `${left}%`, width: `${Math.min(width, 100 - left)}%` }\n  }\n\n  const getNoDateStyle = () => {\n    const today = new Date()\n    const left = (differenceInDays(today, axisStart) / totalDays) * 100\n    return { left: `${left}%`, width: '1.5%' }\n  }\n\n  const todayPosition = (differenceInDays(new Date(), axisStart) / totalDays) * 100\n\n  if (timelineTasks.length === 0) {\n    return (\n      <div className=\"flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-20 text-text-muted\">\n        <CalendarOff size={48} strokeWidth={1.5} className=\"mb-4\" />\n        <p className=\"font-display text-lg font-medium\">暂无任务可显示</p>\n        <p className=\"mt-1 text-sm\">\n          {timelineShowNoDate ? '当前视图没有任务' : '创建带有截止日期的任务以在时间线中显示'}\n        </p>\n        {!timelineShowNoDate && (\n          <button\n            onClick={() => setTimelineShowNoDate(true)}\n            className=\"mt-3 rounded-lg border border-border px-4 py-2 text-sm transition-colors hover:bg-surface-hover\"\n          >\n            显示所有任务\n          </button>\n        )}\n      </div>\n    )\n  }\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"space-y-4\">\n      {/* Toggle */}\n      <div className=\"flex items-center gap-2\">\n        <label className=\"flex cursor-pointer items-center gap-2 text-sm text-text-secondary\">\n          <input\n            type=\"checkbox\"\n            checked={timelineShowNoDate}\n            onChange={(e) => setTimelineShowNoDate(e.target.checked)}\n            className=\"checkbox-done !h-4 !w-4 !rounded-sm\"\n          />\n          显示无截止日期的任务\n        </label>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Legend */}\n      <div className=\"flex items-center gap-4 text-[11px] text-text-muted\">\n        <span className=\"flex items-center gap-1\">\n          <span className=\"inline-block h-2.5 w-6 rounded-sm bg-primary\" /> 已完成\n        </span>\n        <span className=\"flex items-center gap-1\">\n          <span className=\"inline-block h-2.5 w-6 rounded-sm bg-primary/40\" /> 未完成\n        </span>\n        <span className=\"flex items-center gap-1\">\n          <span className=\"inline-block h-2.5 w-6 rounded-sm bg-danger/50\" /> 逾期\n        </span>\n      </div>\n\n      {/* Timeline */}\n      <div className=\"overflow-x-auto rounded-2xl border border-border bg-surface\">\n        <div className=\"min-w-[800px]\">\n          {/* Time axis header */}\n          <div className=\"flex border-b border-border\">\n            {/* Task name column header */}\n            <div className=\"w-56 shrink-0 border-r border-border px-4 py-2\">\n              <span className=\"text-xs font-medium text-text-muted\">任务</span>\n            </div>\n            {/* Time axis */}\n            <div className=\"relative flex-1\">\n              <div className=\"flex\">\n                {weeks.map((weekStart, i) => (\n                  <div\n                    key={i}\n                    className=\"flex-1 border-r border-border-subtle px-1 py-2 text-center text-[11px] text-text-muted\"\n                  >\n                    {format(weekStart, 'M/d', { locale: zhCN })}\n                  </div>\n                ))}\n              </div>\n              {/* Today marker */}\n              {todayPosition >= 0 && todayPosition <= 100 && (\n                <div\n                  className=\"absolute bottom-0 top-0 z-10 w-px bg-danger/60\"\n                  style={{ left: `${todayPosition}%` }}\n                >\n                  <div className=\"absolute -left-3 -top-0.5 text-[9px] font-medium text-danger\">今</div>\n                </div>\n              )}\n            </div>\n          </div>\n\n          {/* Task rows grouped by project */}\n          {groups.map((group, gi) => (\n            <motion.div\n              key={group.name}\n              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}\n              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}\n              transition={{ delay: gi * 0.05 }}\n            >\n              {/* Project group header */}\n              <div className=\"flex border-b border-border-subtle bg-bg/50\">\n                <div className=\"flex w-56 shrink-0 items-center gap-2 border-r border-border px-4 py-2\">\n                  <span\n                    className=\"flex h-5 w-5 items-center justify-center rounded text-xs\"\n                    style={{ backgroundColor: group.color + '20', color: group.color }}\n                  >\n                    {group.icon}\n                  </span>\n                  <span className=\"text-xs font-semibold text-text-secondary\">{group.name}</span>\n                  <span className=\"text-[10px] text-text-muted\">({group.tasks.length})</span>\n                </div>\n                <div className=\"relative flex-1\" />\n              </div>\n\n              {/* Task rows */}\n              {group.tasks.map((task, ti) => {\n                const isDone = task.status === 'done'\n                const isOverdue = task.due_date && isPast(parseISO(task.due_date)) && !isDone && !isToday(parseISO(task.due_date))\n                const hasDueDate = !!task.due_date\n\n                return (\n                  <motion.div\n                    key={task.id}\n                    initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -10 }}\n                    animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}\n                    transition={{ delay: gi * 0.05 + ti * 0.02 }}\n                    className=\"group flex border-b border-border-subtle transition-colors hover:bg-surface-hover\"\n                  >\n                    {/* Task name */}\n                    <div className=\"flex w-56 shrink-0 items-center gap-2 border-r border-border px-4 py-2.5\">\n                      <button\n                        onClick={() => toggleTask(task)}\n                        className=\"shrink-0 text-text-muted transition-colors hover:text-primary\"\n                      >\n                        {isDone ? <CheckCircle2 size={14} className=\"text-success\" /> : <Circle size={14} />}\n                      </button>\n                      <span className={`truncate text-sm ${isDone ? 'text-text-muted line-through' : 'text-text'}`}>\n                        {task.title}\n                      </span>\n                      {isOverdue && <AlertCircle size={12} className=\"shrink-0 text-danger\" />}\n                    </div>\n\n                    {/* Bar area */}\n                    <div className=\"relative flex-1 py-2.5\">\n                      {hasDueDate ? (\n                        <div\n                          className=\"absolute top-1/2 h-5 -translate-y-1/2 rounded-md transition-all\"\n                          style={{\n                            ...getBarStyle(task),\n                            backgroundColor: isDone ? 'var(--color-primary)' : isOverdue ? 'var(--color-danger)' : (group.color || PRIORITY_COLORS[task.priority]),\n                            opacity: isDone ? 0.7 : 0.45,\n                          }}\n                        >\n                          {/* Bar label on hover */}\n                          <div className=\"pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 flex items-center overflow-hidden px-1.5 opacity-0 transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100\">\n                            <span className=\"truncate text-[10px] font-medium text-white drop-shadow\">\n                              {format(parseISO(task.created_at), 'M/d')} → {format(parseISO(task.due_date!), 'M/d')}\n                            </span>\n                          </div>\n                        </div>\n                      ) : (\n                        <div\n                          className=\"absolute top-1/2 h-4 w-3 -translate-y-1/2 rounded-sm bg-text-muted/30\"\n                          style={getNoDateStyle()}\n                          title=\"无截止日期\"\n                        />\n                      )}\n                    </div>\n                  </motion.div>\n                )\n              })}\n            </motion.div>\n          ))}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  )\n}\n",
  "filePath": "/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/src/components/tasks/TaskTimeline.tsx"
}

{
  "filePath": "/home/shy/workspace/taskflow/src/App.tsx",
  "newString": "import { useEffect } from 'react'\nimport { useAppStore } from './store'\nimport { useThemeStore } from './store/theme'\nimport Sidebar from './components/layout/Sidebar'\nimport Header from './components/layout/Header'\nimport TaskList from './components/tasks/TaskList'\nimport TaskTimeline from './components/tasks/TaskTimeline'\nimport TaskForm from './components/tasks/TaskForm'\nimport StatsDashboard from './components/stats/StatsDashboard'\nimport PomodoroTimer from './components/pomodoro/PomodoroTimer'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\n\nexport default function App() {\n  const { currentView, currentProjectId, viewMode, fetchProjects, fetchTags, fetchTasks } = useAppStore()\n  const { theme } = useThemeStore()\n  const [showForm, setShowForm] = useState(false)\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchProjects()\n    fetchTags()\n  }, [])\n\n  // Re-fetch tasks whenever view, project, or viewMode changes\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchTasks()\n  }, [currentView, currentProjectId, viewMode])\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"noise-bg flex h-screen overflow-hidden bg-bg text-text\">\n      <Sidebar />\n      <main className=\"flex flex-1 flex-col overflow-hidden\">\n        <Header onAddTask={() => setShowForm(true)} />\n        <div className=\"flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6\">\n          {currentView === 'stats' ? ## Assistant (Build · mimo-v2-pro · 9.0s)

_Thinking:_

Let me also make sure the checkbox-done style works for the timeline's toggle checkbox. The timeline uses `className="checkbox-done !h-4 !w-4 !rounded-sm"` but the checkbox-done style has `border-radius: 50%` which makes it round. For the toggle, we need a square checkbox. Let me check the CSS and maybe add a separate class.Actually, looking at the CSS:```css
.checkbox-done {
  border-radius: 50%;
}
```This will make the timeline toggle look like a round checkbox. I should either use a different class or override the border-radius. I already used `!rounded-sm` in the className, but since the CSS uses `border-radius: 50%`, the `!important` override with Tailwind should work since Tailwind v4 uses `!important` with the `!` prefix.


The `!rounded-sm` with the `!` prefix in Tailwind v4 will override the `border-radius: 50%` from the CSS, so that should work fine. Now I'll put together a summary of what I've accomplished.

时间线视图功能完成。改动汇总：

| 文件 | 变更 |
|------|------|
| `src/store/index.ts` | 新增 `viewMode`、`timelineShowNoDate` 状态及 setter |
| `src/components/layout/Header.tsx` | 搜索栏旁新增「列表 / 时间线」切换按钮组，仅在任务类视图显示 |
| `src/components/tasks/TaskTimeline.tsx` | **新建** — 甘特图核心组件 |
| `src/App.tsx` | 导入 TaskTimeline，`viewMode` 切换时自动 refetch |

**时间线组件特性：**
- 按项目分组展示任务行
- 横轴按周刻度，红色竖线标记今天
- 条形 = created_at → due_date 的时间跨度
- 颜色区分：实色=已完成、半透明=未完成、红色=逾期
- 悬浮显示日期范围
- 底部开关：显示/隐藏无截止日期任务
- 切换到时间线模式自动扩展日期范围（前1月→后3月）

启动 `npm run dev` 即可体验。
